  I just made minor changes for self-understanding. I don't claim authority of any class.

Data type for a code segment. Can be a regular segment, block of code
segments, a par statement (cobegin/coend) as well as while loops and if
statements.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2984" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Seg"></a><a id="2989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2989" class="Datatype">Seg</a> <a id="2993" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2995" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2999" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="LTL._==n_"></a><a id="4653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4653" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==n_</a>        <a id="4666" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4668" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4669" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4671" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1126" class="Datatype">NVar</a><a id="4677" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4679" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4681" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4682" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4682" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="4684" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4686" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="4687" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4689" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4691" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4079" class="Datatype">LTL</a>     <a id="4699" class="Comment">-- Nat variable x has the value n</a>
  <a id="LTL._==b_"></a><a id="4735" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4735" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==b_</a>        <a id="4748" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4750" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4751" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4751" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1226" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4759" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4761" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4763" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4764" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4764" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4766" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4768" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1226" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4772" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4774" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4776" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4079" class="Datatype">LTL</a>  <a id="4781" class="Comment">-- Bool variable x has the value of y</a>
  <a id="LTL.isTrue"></a><a id="4821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4821" class="InductiveConstructor">isTrue</a>       <a id="4834" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4836" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4837" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4837" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4839" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4841" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1226" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4845" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4847" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4079" class="Datatype">LTL</a>               <a id="4867" class="Comment">-- Variable x has the value -- true</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## The LTL-rule data type

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6790" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="LTLRule"></a><a id="6795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6795" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a> <a id="6803" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6805" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6809" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₁"></a><a id="6817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6817" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₁</a>   <a id="6824" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4079" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6830" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6832" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6795" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6847" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on first element</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₂"></a><a id="6885" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6885" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₂</a>   <a id="6892" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6894" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4079" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6898" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6900" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6795" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6915" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on second element</a>

## Propositional logic representation

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10466" class="Comment">-- Representation of propositional logic</a>
<a id="10507" class="Comment">-- data Props : Set where</a>
<a id="10533" class="Comment">--   T ⊥         : Props</a>
<a id="10558" class="Comment">--   _∧_ _∨_ _⇒_ : Props → Props → Props</a>
<a id="10599" class="Comment">--   p&#39;          : ℕ → Props</a>
<a id="10628" class="Comment">--   ~_          : Props → Props</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Translator

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10701" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Translator"></a><a id="10708" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#10708" class="Module">Translator</a> <a id="10719" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Translator for concurrent programs. Translates program representations into
transition relations (TransRel). The relations keep track of the LTL-formulas
related to the program statements of the programs.

### Actions

Data type for actions, reference to what happened when translating the program

### Hoare-style Triples

Represents transition relations, < pre > action < post >, where pre is the
precondition of the program statement, action the reference to the type of
program statement, and post the postcondition of the statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12077" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="TransRel"></a><a id="12082" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12082" class="Datatype">TransRel</a> <a id="12091" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12093" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="12097" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="TransRel.&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;"></a><a id="12105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;</a> <a id="12113" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12115" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12116" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="12119" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4079" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12124" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12126" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12128" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11053" class="Datatype">Action</a> <a id="12135" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12138" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12138" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="12141" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12143" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4079" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12146" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12148" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12082" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>  <a id="12160" class="Comment">-- Hoare-style Triple</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translates a program statement into the corresponding `TransRel`.
  * `l`: Program label of the program statement.
  * `Stm`: The program statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="transStm"></a><a id="12358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12358" class="Function">transStm</a> <a id="12367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1009" class="Datatype">Label</a> <a id="12375" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2509" class="Datatype">Stm</a> <a id="12381" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12383" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12082" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

Flattens a list of lists into a single list.

Converts a list of segments and a label, representing a single block segment,
into a list of `TransRel`. The result contains the representation of the program
flow.

* `p`: Label of the parent segment.
* `List Seg`: List of all child segments.

Converts a list of segments into a single `LTL`. The list represents all child
segments initiated by a parent `par` segment. The result is an `LTL` used as a
precondition in order to allow the parent segment to be considered executed.

Helper function for translate that uses different translation approaches
depending on the type of segment to be translated.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15290" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="15294" class="Keyword">TERMINATING</a> <a id="15306" class="Symbol">#-}</a> <a id="15310" class="Comment">-- used to guarantee that there is no infinite looping</a>

  <a id="16779" class="Comment">-- Translate the if statement</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translate function that takes a program and returns a list of TransRel.
The list consists of two parts, first the statement specific translations,
the second the program flow relations between the segments.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="translate"></a><a id="17043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#17043" class="Function">translate</a> <a id="17053" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3847" class="Record">Prog</a> <a id="17060" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17062" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.List.html#80" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="17067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12082" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

## Rules to construct proofs

Contains rules to use when construction proofs. Also has functions to check if
rules are used legally. Used in ProofChecker

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17332" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Rules"></a><a id="17339" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#17339" class="Module">Rules</a> <a id="17345" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Data type for program rules, indexed with rule and `LTL`. Specifically for
proof-steps regarding the programs

                                             <a id="18236" class="Comment">-- control progression</a>
